Title: Uninstantiated Properties Exist

Position:
Properties can exist even when nothing has them. The property of being a unicorn exists.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-006
Work: Unknown
Title: Determinism vs Randomness vs Unpredictability

Position:
Determinism, randomness, and predictability are distinct concepts that must not be conflated.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-007
Work: Unknown
Title: Personal Identity Through Time

Position:
Personal identity consists in psychological continuity, not bodily continuity.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-008
Work: Unknown
Title: Causality as Counterfactual Dependence

Position:
Event A causes event B iff: (1) both occur, and (2) had A not occurred, B would not have occurred.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: METPH-001
Work: Unknown
Title: Bundle Theory of Personal Identity

Position:
A person/self is class of all mental contents I-related to given mental content. Two mental contents belong to same person iff there is chain such that each link directly interacts with its neighbor. Direct interaction = no intervening physical events.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: METPH-002
Work: Unknown
Title: Content-Bearing Processes Are Ipso Facto Mental

Position:
If physical process non-derivatively bears representational/thematic content, it is ipso facto mental (whatever else it is). Content-bearing is sufficient (though not necessary) for mentality.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-011
Work: Unknown
Title: Binary Truth Despite Continuous Representation

Position:
AI systems demonstrate that truth remains fundamentally binary (true/false) even though cognitive systems represent information continuously. Continuous confidence values or fuzzy representations are epistemic features, not ontological features of truth itself.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-012
Work: Unknown
Title: Causation as the Essence of Temporal Precedence

Position:
For one event e to precede another event e* is for there to be a possible causal process beginning with e and ending with e*. Simultaneity is the absence of such a process.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-013
Work: Unknown
Title: Continuity as the Essence of Causation

Position:
Effects are continuations of their causes. Causation essentially involves continuity - causal processes preserve structural relationships across temporal intervals without gaps.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-014
Work: Unknown
Title: Causation a Relation Between Events, Not Objects

Position:
Causation is fundamentally a relation between events, not between objects. Objects participate in causal relations only derivatively, in virtue of events involving those objects.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-015
Work: Unknown
Title: Conditions Identical with Event-Patterns

Position:
Conditions are identical with event-patterns. A condition is not a state but rather a pattern or type of event sequence that can be instantiated multiple times.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-016
Work: Unknown
Title: So-Called Changes Typically Identical with Meta-Changes

Position:
What are ordinarily called changes are typically meta-changes - changes in the rate, direction, or pattern of already-occurring changes rather than absolute transitions from rest to motion or vice versa.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-017
Work: Unknown
Title: Threshold Effects and Psychological Overdetermination

Position:
In psychology, causation often involves exceeding thresholds rather than simple sufficient conditions. An effect may require the confluence of multiple reasons, none sufficient alone but jointly sufficient once a threshold is exceeded.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-018
Work: Unknown
Title: Threshold Effects and the Analog-Digital Distinction

Position:
Discontinuous changes tend to involve threshold effects; continuous changes do not. To the extent the world changes discontinuously it has digital structure; to the extent continuously, analog structure.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-019
Work: Unknown
Title: Causes as INUS-Conditions

Position:
In most contexts, to say 'X caused Y' means 'X was an INUS condition for Y' - an Insufficient but Non-redundant part of an Unnecessary but Sufficient condition for Y's occurrence.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-020
Work: Unknown
Title: Counterfactuals Hold in Virtue of Dependence-Relations

Position:
All counterfactuals affirm the existence of instances of necessitation of some kind. Causal counterfactuals hold in virtue of causal dependence-relations; logical counterfactuals hold in virtue of logical dependence-relations.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-021
Work: Unknown
Title: David Lewis's Possible Worlds Analysis of Counterfactuals Rejected

Position:
David Lewis's analysis of counterfactuals in terms of similar possible worlds is false. Events have deep causal roots such that changing one event requires either massive world-differences or changes to deterministic mechanisms.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-022
Work: Unknown
Title: Program-Causality Distinguished from Token-Causality

Position:
Program-causality differs from token-causality. Sometimes the appropriate causal explanation cites a condition that guaranteed occurrence of token-causes rather than the token-causes themselves.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-023
Work: Unknown
Title: Causal Redundancy Defeats Counterfactual Analysis

Position:
Where there is causal redundancy, causal truths cannot be converted into counterfactual truths. 'X caused Y' can be true even when 'if X hadn't occurred, Y wouldn't have occurred' is false.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-028
Work: Unknown
Title: Necessary Truths Don't Describe the Empirical World

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-029
Work: Unknown
Title: Transcendental Deduction of World-Structure from Coherent Experience

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-030
Work: Unknown

Position:
To be at rest is to fail to move during a non-null interval; an object at a point during its motion is not at rest

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-031
Work: Unknown

Position:
Any finite number can be represented as sum of infinite series; any case of motion involves traversing infinitely many finite distances in finite time

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-032
Work: Unknown

Position:
Space-time regions do not themselves have places; they are constituents, not occupants, of space-time

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-033
Work: Unknown

Position:
For x to cause y is for y to be a continuation of x, not for x-like events to always precede y-like events

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-034
Work: Unknown

Position:
Continuity represents preservation; discontinuity represents ex nihilo change

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-035
Work: Unknown

Position:
The legitimacy of inference from cause to effect lies in the irrationality of positing spontaneities

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-036
Work: Unknown
Title: Eternal matter vs. creation ex nihilo

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-037
Work: Unknown
Title: Pre-Civilizational Perception as Direct and Natural

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-038
Work: Unknown
Title: Modal Realism's Ontological Extravagance

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-039
Work: Unknown
Title: Essentialism and Modal Knowledge

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-040
Work: Unknown
Title: Space-Time Structure and Modality

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-41
Work: Unknown
Title: Truth is discovered, not made

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-42
Work: Unknown
Title: Knowledge is a subject-object relationship; truth is objective

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MP-072
Work: Unknown
Title: Cardinal Numbers as Classes of Ordered Pairs

Position:
For any cardinal n, n can be identified with class Cn of all ordered pairs <Kn#,Rn#> where Kn# is any class and Rn# any relation such that class k has n-many members iff kRn#Kn#. Reconciles Frege and Von Neumann.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-055
Work: Unknown
Title: Modified Cartesian Position on Temporal Consciousness

Position:
The thinking subject exists essentially as a temporal being, not merely as a being located in time. The ego cogito experiences duration from within, not as an external temporal container but as the very structure of conscious experience itself. Time's apparent passage might be neither objective feature of reality nor mere illusion, but rather the form under which reality necessarily appears to finite conscious subjects.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-056
Work: Unknown
Title: Manifest Image and Scientific Image Relationship

Position:
McTaggart's argument opens onto fundamental questions about the relationship between subjective experience and objective reality, between the manifest and scientific images of the world. Its enduring significance lies in its demonstration that rigorous conceptual analysis can reveal deep structural problems in our most basic metaphysical commitments—problems that resist easy dissolution and point toward the need for more sophisticated philosophical frameworks that can accommodate both the demands of logical rigor and the irreducible character of conscious temporal experience.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: META-057
Work: Unknown
Title: The B-Series is Generated by Change

Position:
The B-series is not opposed to change; it is generated by change. When A occurs, B is not yet occurring; when B occurs, C is not yet occurring. Change produces succession, and succession produces the B-series. Its unchanging order is the outcome of the generative process, not evidence of stasis. The 'now' is simply the boundary between what has been generated and what has not yet been generated.


================================================================================
DOMAIN: METH (12 positions)
================================================================================

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: METH-007
Work: Unknown
Title: AI Construction Tests Cognitive Theories Empirically

Position:
The requirement that cognitive theories be implementable in functioning AI systems provides an empirical constraint: theories that cannot generate working systems are falsified. This connects abstract theorizing to concrete engineering requirements.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: METH-008
Work: Unknown
Title: Formalization Requires Generative Not Just Organizational Adequacy

Position:
AI reveals that adequate formalization requires not just organizing existing knowledge but generating new valid instances. A formalization is adequate only if it can generate the full range of valid cases, not merely classify them post hoc.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: METH-009
Work: Unknown
Title: Generative Tests Reveal Hidden Inadequacies in Formalizations

Position:
Testing whether a formalization can generate valid new instances (as AI systems must) reveals inadequacies invisible to purely organizational approaches. Many traditional formalizations fail this stronger generative test. **PHILOSOPHY OF AI (1 positions): AI-004 to AI-004**

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: METH-010
Work: Unknown
Title: No Such Thing as Enumerative Induction

Position:
There is no such thing as enumerative induction (inferring 'all Fs are Gs' from 'all observed Fs are Gs'). What appears to be enumerative induction always involves implicit appeal to Inference to the Best Explanation (IBE).

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: METH-011
Work: Unknown
Title: Discontinuity-Elimination the Essence of Explanation

Position:
To explain is to eliminate discontinuities. A correct scientific hypothesis eliminates anomalies by showing how apparently disconnected facts are part of continuous causal processes.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: METH-012
Work: Unknown
Title: Inductive Knowledge as Knowledge of Continuities

Position:
Inductive knowledge is knowledge of continuities between continuities. Valid induction extends known continuous causal processes to unobserved cases by identifying higher-order patterns of continuity.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: METH-013
Work: Unknown
Title: IBE Justified by Continuity-Completion

Position:
Inference to the Best Explanation (IBE) is justified because it completes causal continuities. A hypothesis is justified to the extent it fills gaps in causal sequences, eliminating discontinuities in the data.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: METH-014
Work: Unknown
Title: Measurement Distinct from Enumeration

Position:
Measurement is fundamentally distinct from enumeration. Length cannot be determined by counting because (1) there are no minimal length units, and (2) length is not strictly additive at large scales.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: METH-015
Work: Unknown
Title: Relativization to Standards the Essence of Measurement

Position:
The essence of measurement is comparison with respect to a standard. All measurement, including 'absolute' measurement, is fundamentally relative comparison to stipulated standards.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: METH-016
Work: Unknown
Title: Three Axioms of Measurement Theory

Position:
Three axioms are necessary for any viable measurement system: (i) If L1>L2 and L2>L3, then L1>L3 (transitivity). (ii) If L1≠L2, one is greater (trichotomy). (iii) If L1=L2 and L2=L3, then L1=L3 (transitivity of identity). Violation makes measurement meaningless.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: METH-017
Work: Unknown
Title: Metrical Conventionalism Versus Strict Conventionalism

Position:
Conventionalism (laws are convention-based) differs from strict conventionalism (laws are convention-determined). Only the former is correct. That laws are expressed relative to conventional standards doesn't make them entirely conventional.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: METH-018
Work: Unknown
Title: Conventionalism Self-Defeating

Position:
Conventionalism is self-defeating. If laws hold in virtue of non-conventional relations between conventions and events (as conventionalism requires), then measurement standard choice is constrained by objective facts, undermining conventionalism. **PHILOSOPHY OF SCIENCE (24 positions): SCI-010 to SCI-055**

ID: METH-005
Work: WORK-012
Title: Cell Biology Analogy Supports Collective-First Methodology

Position:
Just as individual cells are better understood in terms of their role in multicellular organisms rather than as autonomous individuals pursuing their own survival, individual humans are better understood in terms of their roles in human collectives. Cell-individualism can be explained in terms of cell-collectivism, but not vice versa; similarly for person-individualism and person-collectivism.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: METH-006
Work: WORK-012
Title: Collective Behavior Cannot Be Explained by Individualist Assumptions

Position:
It is very difficult to explain group behavior - whether mobs or advanced cultures - on the assumption that collectives represent averages of behaviors of autonomous individual deciders. Outside of contexts with immediate physical threats or prospects of crude gratification, people give far too much weight to existing beliefs and mores in far too well-defined ways to be accounted for by individualist hypotheses.

ID: MIND-019

Work: Unknown
Title: Conceptual Atomism Is False

Position:
Fodor's conceptual atomism (concepts have no constitutive interdependencies) is demonstrably false.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-021
Work: Unknown
Title: Constitutive Relations Are Not Containment Relations

Position:
Constitutive connections among concepts are not containment relations or decomposability relations (following Wittgenstein). Azure is constitutively related to navy blue but neither contains the other.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-022
Work: Unknown
Title: Symbol Containment Theory Leads to Thinking Absurdities

Position:
If concepts were symbols and constitutive relations were containment relations, thinking about 1,423 would require simultaneously thinking about 1,422, 1,421, etc. This is absurd.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-023
Work: Unknown
Title: Thought Is Not Computation Over Symbols

Position:
Mental activity does not consist in computation or processing of internal symbolic code. Cognitive activity is not fundamentally information processing over a language-like medium.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-024
Work: Unknown
Title: We Are Not Computers (Consequence)

Position:
If there is no Language of Thought, and if being a computer requires internal symbolic processing (standard characterization), then we are not computers.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-025
Work: Unknown
Title: No Bare Representation: Aspectual Constraint

Position:
One cannot just represent an object without representing it AS having properties. All representation is aspectual.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-026
Work: Unknown
Title: Properties Individuated by Relations to Other Properties

Position:
All properties are individuated, at least in part, by their relations to other properties. Grasping any property requires ability to locate it in 'space' of other properties.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-027
Work: Unknown
Title: Color Concepts Require Multiple Color Grasp

Position:
Cannot grasp specific color/shade without ability to grasp other colors. Creature that can represent only one shade cannot represent what's specific about that shade.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-028
Work: Unknown
Title: Mental Interaction Has Normative Dimension

Position:
When mental contents interact, result is thematically/semantically appropriate to interacting contents. This appropriateness has no analogue in purely physical interactions. Mental interaction is explicative, not merely causal.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-039
Work: Unknown
Title: Functional Replication Reveals Necessary Architecture

Position:
When AI successfully replicates a cognitive function, the architecture required for that replication reveals necessary (though not necessarily sufficient) conditions for that function. This provides insight into the minimal requirements for cognition.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-040
Work: Unknown
Title: Music Has Cognitive Architecture Parallel to Language

Position:
AI analysis reveals that music processing requires cognitive architecture with structural parallels to language: hierarchical organization, syntactic rules, and semantic interpretation. This supports the view that music is a cognitive system with language-like properties.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-041
Work: Unknown
Title: Musical Competence Requires Innate Structure

Position:
AI systems that successfully generate or analyze music require substantial innate architectural constraints, suggesting that human musical competence also depends on innate cognitive structure rather than being purely learned.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-042
Work: Unknown
Title: Connectionism Can Implement Chomskyan Insights

Position:
Contrary to Chomsky's critique, connectionist AI systems can implement key Chomskyan insights about innate linguistic structure. The debate is not whether innate structure exists but how it is implemented - symbolic rules vs. weighted connections.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-043
Work: Unknown
Title: AI Falsifies Classical Computational Theory of Mind

Position:
The success of modern AI systems (especially neural networks) falsifies the classical computational theory of mind which requires serial symbol manipulation. Intelligence can be achieved through parallel, subsymbolic processes that don't manipulate discrete symbols according to explicit rules.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-044
Work: Unknown
Title: Intelligence Does Not Require Symbol Manipulation

Position:
AI demonstrates that intelligence and rational behavior do not require manipulation of discrete symbols in a language of thought. Subsymbolic pattern recognition and transformation can achieve cognitive competence without symbolic representation.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-045
Work: Unknown
Title: Analog Computation Can Support Rational Thought

Position:
Neural network AI systems demonstrate that analog (continuous) computation can support rational thought and problem-solving, contrary to the classical assumption that rationality requires discrete digital computation.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-046
Work: Unknown
Title: Neural Architecture Constrains Cognitive Possibilities

Position:
AI neural architectures reveal that cognitive capacities are constrained by underlying computational architecture. Different architectures enable different cognitive possibilities, suggesting mind is fundamentally shaped by its neural implementation.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-047
Work: Unknown
Title: Multiple Realizability Has Architectural Limits

Position:
While cognitive functions show some multiple realizability, AI reveals that architectural constraints limit which substrates can implement which functions. This challenges strong multiple realizability theses that treat implementation as irrelevant to function.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-048
Work: Unknown
Title: Domain-General Principles Underlie Domain-Specific Competencies

Position:
AI systems demonstrate that apparently domain-specific competencies (language, music) can arise from application of domain-general computational principles to different types of input. This supports a middle ground between pure modularity and pure domain-generality.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-049
Work: Unknown
Title: Consciousness Has Functional Role Absent in Current AI

Position:
AI systems demonstrate that many cognitive functions traditionally associated with consciousness (perception, reasoning, learning) can occur without consciousness. This reveals consciousness has a distinct functional role that current AI lacks - likely related to unified subjective experience and certain forms of self-monitoring.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-050
Work: Unknown
Title: AI Success Without Consciousness Reveals Consciousness is Not Required for Intelligence

Position:
The success of AI at intelligent tasks without consciousness demonstrates that consciousness is not necessary for intelligence per se, but may be necessary for specific types of cognitive integration or self-awareness.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-051
Work: Unknown
Title: Phenomenal Consciousness vs Functional Consciousness Distinction

Position:
AI reveals a crucial distinction between phenomenal consciousness (subjective experience) and functional consciousness (information integration, self-monitoring). AI can have functional analogs without phenomenal properties.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-052
Work: Unknown
Title: Self-Representation Requires Specific Architectural Features

Position:
AI systems reveal that genuine self-representation requires specific architectural features: recursive self-modeling, distinction between self and environment, and temporal continuity tracking. Not all intelligent systems automatically have these features.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-053
Work: Unknown
Title: Narrative Self vs Minimal Self in AI Architecture

Position:
AI demonstrates the distinction between minimal self (basic subject of experience) and narrative self (autobiographical self-concept). These require different architectural implementations and can exist independently. **PHILOSOPHY OF SCIENCE (6 positions): SCI-004 to SCI-009**

ID: AI-002
Work: WORK-011
Title: Classical vs. AI Computing Architecture Alignment

Position:
Classical logic's properties (explicit rules, step-by-step deduction, binary truth values, context-independence, compositional semantics) match classical computing architecture. System L's properties (flexible search, pattern-based reasoning, degrees of plausibility, context-sensitivity, holistic processing) align with AI systems.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: AI-003
Work: WORK-011
Title: AI Vindicates Non-Revisionist Epistemology

Position:
AI operation provides empirical support for non-revisionist epistemology that accepts knowledge about unobservables/future/counterfactuals, recognizes necessary integration of empirical and rational components, understands theoretical knowledge as based on causal mechanisms and continuity, rejects pure empiricism while maintaining importance of empirical evidence.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: AI-004
Work: Unknown
Title: AI Provides Empirical Test for Logical Theories

Position:
Artificial intelligence systems, particularly large language models, provide empirical evidence about how reasoning actually works, revealing that System L's approach better captures both human and artificial reasoning than classical logic.

Position:

ID: LANG-024

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: LANG-025
Work: WORK-008
Title: Names as Concept-Laden Labels

Position:
Names are mere labels (non-descriptive), as Kripke argued, but labels 'pick up' descriptive information through how one learns their reference. Semantics (what expressions literally mean) differs from knowledge of semantics (how meaning is known), and this difference explains apparent descriptive content.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: LANG-026
Work: WORK-008
Title: Co-referential Names Can Differ in Meaning

Position:
'Superman' and 'Clark Kent' differ in meaning despite co-referring. 'Superman is in the building' says that a certain property-set (superhuman strength, flight ability, etc.) is uniquely instantiated and any such instance is in the building. 'Clark Kent is in the building' says a different property-set (reporter, wears glasses, etc.) is uniquely instantiated.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: LANG-027

Position:

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Position:
Constitutive connections among concepts are not containment relations or decomposability relations (following Wittgenstein). Azure is constitutively related to navy blue but neither contains the other.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-022
Work: Unknown

Position:
If concepts were symbols and constitutive relations were containment relations, thinking about 1,423 would require simultaneously thinking about 1,422, 1,421, etc. This is absurd.

Position:

ID: MIND-030
Work: WORK-011
Title: Intelligence is Fundamentally Analog Not Digital

Position:

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-031
Work: WORK-011
Title: Connectionism Over Computational Theory

Position:
Modern AI based on neural networks aligns much more closely with connectionist theories than with computational theory of mind. Systems process information through patterns of activation across networks of weighted connections, operating fundamentally continuously rather than discretely.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-032
Work: WORK-011
Title: Consciousness Serves Survival Functions

Position:
Consciousness in biological organisms serves specific functional roles: real-time environmental monitoring, reflexive self-awareness, integration of multiple cognitive processes, immediate damage prevention, action guidance. Current AI lacks these because it doesn't need them—operates in controlled environments without survival pressure.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-033
Work: WORK-011
Title: Consciousness-Like Features Require Unified Real-Time Processing

Position:
Implementing consciousness-like features in AI would require: unified workspaces for real-time integration of multiple data streams, immediate damage-prevention systems analogous to pain, action-guiding systems analogous to emotions. These differ fundamentally from biological consciousness but serve similar functional roles.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-034
Work: WORK-011
Title: Self as Emergent Hierarchical Organization

Position:
Self/ego exists but is best understood as emergent property of pre-existing cognitive processes. Various thoughts/perceptions/emotions organized into hierarchies based on survival value. What we call 'self' is this hierarchical organization; 'sense of self' mediates between awareness of external events and internal states.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: MIND-035
Work: WORK-011
Title: Cohesion Relations in AI Minds

Position:

These provide precise models of binding principles uniting mental contents.

The phenomenology of experience has irreducible epistemic significance.

================================================================================
DOMAIN: PHILOSOPHY_OF_SCIENCE (45 positions)
================================================================================

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-001
Work: WORK-008
Title: Confirmation Requires Principled Generalizations

Position:
Only principled (nomic/causal) generalizations, not accidental generalizations, can be confirmed. When 'All ravens are black' is read as a principled generalization, it has nomic content and is not equivalent to 'All non-black things are non-ravens.'

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-002
Work: WORK-011
Title: AI Systems Test Philosophical Theories Empirically

Position:
Philosophical theories about reasoning, knowledge acquisition, scientific discovery can be empirically tested by examining whether successful AI systems operate according to those theories. AI provides concrete examinable implementations allowing theory adjudication.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-003
Work: WORK-011
Title: Logic of Discovery is Possible

Position:
Contrary to traditional philosophy of science claiming logic of discovery is impossible, examining AI scientific reasoning reveals identifiable principles guiding successful theory generation. Genuine logic of discovery exists.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-004
Work: Unknown
Title: AI Falsifies Popperian Falsificationism

Position:
AI's success in scientific discovery falsifies Popper's theory that science proceeds primarily through conjecture and refutation. AI systems generate successful theories through pattern matching and inductive generalization, not primarily through bold conjectures and attempts at falsification.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-005
Work: Unknown
Title: Inductive Discovery Precedes Deductive Testing

Position:
Contra Popper, successful scientific discovery requires inductive pattern recognition to generate plausible hypotheses before deductive testing. AI demonstrates that purely conjectural approaches without inductive guidance are ineffective.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-006
Work: Unknown
Title: Reverse Brain Engineering as Scientific Method

Position:
By building AI systems that replicate cognitive functions, we can infer the computational architecture necessary for those functions. This 'reverse engineering' of the brain through AI construction represents a new and powerful methodology in philosophy of science and cognitive science.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-007
Work: Unknown
Title: AI Falsifies Deductive-Nomological Model of Explanation

Position:
AI's successful explanatory practices falsify the deductive-nomological (covering law) model of explanation. AI generates successful explanations through pattern recognition, analogy, and causal modeling that don't require deduction from universal laws.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-008
Work: Unknown
Title: Causal-Mechanistic Explanation Doesn't Require Universal Laws

Position:
AI demonstrates that causal-mechanistic explanation can be successful without appeal to universal laws. Understanding how something works doesn't require subsuming it under exceptionless generalizations.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-009
Work: Unknown
Title: Explanatory Understanding Through Pattern Recognition

Position:
AI reveals that explanatory understanding can be achieved through recognition of patterns and structural similarities rather than derivation from laws. This suggests explanation is more about grasping relevant relationships than deductive systematization.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-010
Work: Unknown
Title: Laws of Nature Not Confined to Actual Objects

Position:
The scope of natural law is not confined to actual or even possible objects. Many laws hold with respect to classes all of whose members are merely possible or even prohibited by other natural laws.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-011
Work: Unknown
Title: Knowledge of Imperceptibles Identical with Conditional Knowledge

Position:
Knowledge of the imperceptible is identical with knowledge of conditional truth. Knowledge of future, past, possible, and imperceptible present states is always conditional knowledge based on laws.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-012
Work: Unknown
Title: Three Kinds of Imperceptibles

Position:
Physical objects can be imperceptible in three ways: (1) imperceptible due to severed causal processes (objects in other rooms); (2) imperceptible due to size but perceptible with technology (cells, molecules); (3) imperceptible by natural law regardless of technology (photons, subatomic particles).

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-013
Work: Unknown
Title: The Epistemic Function of Natural Law

Position:
Scientists aspire to identify natural laws so they can, when given context-specific information, make true statements about future, past, or possible behavior of contexts. Laws enable conditional prediction and explanation.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-014
Work: Unknown
Title: Science Prioritizes Principles Over Particular Facts

Position:
Any interest science has in a given particular fact is subordinate to its interest in the general principles in terms of which that fact is to be understood. Scientists study particular instances only insofar as they instantiate general laws.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-015
Work: Unknown
Title: Laws May Be Place and Time-Sensitive

Position:
Some natural laws are place- and time-sensitive rather than spatiotemporally invariant. Laws need not hold uniformly across all regions of space-time to be genuine laws.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-016
Work: Unknown
Title: Hume's Regularity Analysis of Causation Is False

Position:
Hume's Regularity Analysis - the view that causation is nothing but constant conjunction, that 'X causes Y' means 'events of type X are regularly followed by events of type Y' - is demonstrably false.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-017
Work: Unknown
Title: Hume-Worlds Observationally Different from Non-Humean Worlds

Position:
A Hume-world (where causation equals regularity with no underlying powers) would be observationally different from our world. The concept of a Hume-world cannot support Hume's analysis.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-018
Work: Unknown
Title: The Deductive-Nomological Model of Explanation Is False

Position:
The Deductive-Nomological (DN) model - which holds that to explain event E is to derive E from natural laws plus antecedent conditions - is fundamentally mistaken. Explanation requires causal knowledge, not merely law-subsumption.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-019
Work: Unknown
Title: DN Viciously Circular via Counterfactual Support

Position:
The DN model is viciously circular if it requires laws to support counterfactuals (as Hempel proposes). Counterfactuals are cryptocausal statements; knowing them requires knowing causes; but knowing causes already provides explanations.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-020
Work: Unknown
Title: Causal Knowledge as Differential Knowledge

Position:
Causal knowledge is differential knowledge - knowledge of what varies with what. To know causes is to know which changes depend on which other changes and in what proportions.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-021
Work: Unknown
Title: Causation as Proportionality Restoration

Position:
Causation is fundamentally proportionality restoration. Effects are proportional to their causes (threshold effects aside). When a force acts on an object, the resulting change is proportional to the force magnitude.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-022
Work: Unknown

Title: Too-Big-To-Fail Paradox

Position:
When financial institutions become so large that their failure would catastrophically damage the economy, they must be either regulated more stringently or broken up. Their size creates moral hazard: they can take excessive risks knowing government must rescue them.

ID: POL-013
Work: WORK-017
Title: 'Intentions of the Framers' Denotes Idealization Not Empirical Reality

Position:
When we speak of 'the intentions of the framers', we are committed to an idealization rather than empirical actuality. The various framers (Adams, Jefferson, Washington) had numerically and qualitatively different minds, so talk of their collective intentions is institutional rather than psychological.

ID: POL-014
Work: WORK-017
Title: Originalism Involves Vicious Circularity

Position:
Originalism collapses into circularity (or triviality): Constitutional interpretations are to be evaluated in terms of framers' intentions, but the framers' intentions are to be understood in terms of the historical and social role of Constitutional interpretation.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: POL-015
Work: WORK-017
Title: Framers' Intentions as Theoretical Constructs Presupposing Conceptions of Constitutionality

Position:
The expression 'intentions of the framers' denotes an idealization—a theoretical construct with no precise spatiotemporal counterpart. The theories embodied in uses of this expression concern the role the Constitution should have, so originalism is viciously circular or trivial.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: POL-016
Work: WORK-017
Title: Counterfactuals About Framers Presuppose Rather Than Ground Constitutional Interpretations

Position:
When legal theorists run counterfactuals about what Jefferson would have said about contemporary issues (like gay marriage), they are not making empirical statements but a priori propositions about what he should have said given his values. This presupposes rather than grounds conceptions of Constitutionality.

ID: POL-017

Position:

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: POL-018

Position:

Title: The Republic as conservative propaganda disguised as political philosophy

Position:
What Plato is discussing in the Republic is not the philosopher's ideal society, or some abstract notion of justice, or the human good. What Plato is discussing is the class-relations of Athenian society, and he is doing so in such a way as to rationalize the existing class-divisions.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: POL-43
Work: Unknown
Title: Plato's Good/Real equivalence as coded social stability doctrine

Position:
In the Republic, Plato also links 'the Good' with 'the real': which makes no sense if taken literally... But Plato is really speaking in code... The 'good'--i.e. the 'real'--is what conduces to social stability; and 'the bad'--i.e. the 'mere shadows'--are what threaten social stability.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: POL-44
Work: Unknown
Title: Plato's political philosophy replaces world with thought-world

Position:
Consider Plato, as he is a paradigm case of a political philosopher. Plato's system was completely a priori... He was really talking about how to replace the world with a world of his own—a world that had little reality, and little justification, outside of his own thought-space.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: POL-45
Work: Unknown
Title: Philosopher-king doctrine is incoherent

Position:
The incoherent idea that society should be ruled by a philosopher king— incoherent, because societies are to be run by sapient doers, not sapient thinkers--- by people who do not flee from the world into intellectual constructions.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: POL-46
Work: Unknown
Title: Marx's political philosophy as destructive a priori fantasy

Position:
Marx... was talking, quite explicitly, about destroying the existing social structure and replacing it with one that had no real basis---other than a totally fabricated one---in reality, and which, when it was implemented, led to loss of life and opportunity on an unprecedented scale.

ID: PP-124

Title: Appeals Process as Ritual Audit Not Truth-Seeking

Position:

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PP-125
Work: Unknown

Position:

Work: Unknown

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-037
Work: Unknown
Title: 𝜉 (Xi) Metric: Price-Fundamental Correlation in Equities

Position:
Introduced proprietary metric 𝜉 (xi) measuring statistical degree to which changes in price correlate with changes in company fundamentals. For large-cap equities, 𝜉 is effectively zero - prices move independently of economic reality.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-038
Work: Unknown
Title: Large-Cap Price Decoupling from Fundamentals

Position:
Large-cap stock prices can rise or fall independently of any measurable change in core economic reality. Fundamental information becomes lagging background noise in markets dominated by order book dynamics, momentum patterns, and algorithmic traders.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-039
Work: Unknown
Title: Why Small and Mid-Cap Show Higher 𝜉

Position:
Smaller firms exhibit modestly higher 𝜉 because: (1) reduced algorithmic saturation, (2) greater transparency of fundamentals, (3) lower narrative interference, (4) analyst neglect paradox allows real performance to move price.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-040
Work: Unknown
Title: Markets Price Second-Order Beliefs Not Value

Position:
When 𝜉 is low, price reflects second-order beliefs (beliefs about what others believe) rather than about what is true. This reflexivity feeds a feedback loop in which narrative and structure supplant content.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-041
Work: Unknown
Title: Stocks as Claims on Imagined Futures Not Intrinsic Utility

Position:
Unlike commodities with intrinsic utility (wheat, copper), stocks are claims on imagined futures with no intrinsic use, only expectations. Their price depends on mood, narrative, and belief - making them more like luxury goods than commodities.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-042
Work: Unknown
Title: OCD as Adaptive Machinery in Overdrive

Position:
OCD is not just pathology but adaptive machinery pushed into overdrive. Built from traits that in right amounts helped ancestors survive: error detection, threat anticipation, long-range consequence modeling, rule-following, mental rehearsal, moral self-monitoring.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-043
Work: Unknown
Title: OCD Prototype in Prehistoric Context

Position:
50,000 years ago in tight-knit band, someone who double-checked perimeter, insisted on ritual cleanliness, mentally simulated threats repeatedly, felt guilty after minor transgressions might have been liability in some ways but godsend in others - especially if compulsions aligned with group needs.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-044
Work: Unknown
Title: OCD as Misapplied Boundary-Maintenance System

Position:
In modern abstract, crowded, digital world, machinery that maintained physical/moral boundaries has no natural object. So turns inward, fixates on trivialities, creates imagined scenarios to defuse through ritual. System isn't broken - it's misapplied, doing its job too well in wrong context.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-045
Work: Unknown
Title: OCD as Sacred Function Misfiring

Position:
You don't get OCD from nowhere - you get it from same architecture that in another life might have made you priest, scout, healer, watchman. Pain is real but mind isn't broken - it's just tuned for world that no longer exists.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-046
Work: Unknown
Title: Economics Not Self-Contained Predictive System

Position:
Economics is not self-contained system that can predict itself. It's downstream of culture, politics, religion, personality, invention. Charismatic leader can redirect nation's economy in week. War, famine, singularity make mockery of best economic models. These events aren't noise - they're constitutive.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-047
Work: Unknown
Title: Economics vs Biology: Probabilistic vs Non-Self-Predictive

Position:
Biology is probabilistic but not arbitrary - state variables constrain future through non-random mechanisms. Economics not even robustly probabilistic. System never was self-predictive to begin with. Not that it's sound but occasionally disrupted - it's that it was never self-predictive.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-048
Work: Unknown
Title: Inca Example: Economics Records But Doesn't Explain Non-Economic Systems

Position:
To predict Inca behavior in 1457, look at 1456 rituals, laws, cosmic beliefs, cosmological metaphors - not marginal utility curves. Economics may record food stores and track trade but won't tell why workers redeployed to sacred site, surplus burned instead of stored, labor restructured to appease eclipse.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-049
Work: Unknown
Title: Serial Killerdom as Specific Cognitive-Behavioral Protocol

Position:
Serial murder is not random violence but premeditated, patterned, highly stylized behavior with limited recurring types (organized/disorganized, visionary/hedonistic, power/mission-oriented). This taxonomic stability suggests it's specific cognitive-behavioral protocol, not generic trauma response.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-050
Work: Unknown
Title: Serial Killerdom Not Modern Invention But Modern Category

Position:
Serial murder has long existed (Gilles de Rais, Elizabeth Báthory, slaughtering priests of empires). What's new isn't behavior but recognition as distinct category - product of modern bureaucratic state with tools to track, name, mythologize recurring patterns.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-051
Work: Unknown
Title: Trauma as Trigger Not Cause of Serial Killing

Position:
Many serial killers had disturbing upbringings but 'trauma = serial killer' doesn't track. Most abuse victims don't become serial murderers. Some notorious killers didn't experience abuse exceeding ordinary dysfunction. Trauma is trigger sparking very particular pre-existing architecture.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-052
Work: Unknown
Title: Serial Killerdom as Evolutionary Spandrel or Vestigial Adaptation

Position:

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-042
Work: Unknown
Title: OCD as Adaptive Machinery in Overdrive

Position:
OCD is not just pathology but adaptive machinery pushed into overdrive. Built from traits that in right amounts helped ancestors survive: error detection, threat anticipation, long-range consequence modeling, rule-following, mental rehearsal, moral self-monitoring.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-043
Work: Unknown
Title: OCD Prototype in Prehistoric Context

Position:
50,000 years ago in tight-knit band, someone who double-checked perimeter, insisted on ritual cleanliness, mentally simulated threats repeatedly, felt guilty after minor transgressions might have been liability in some ways but godsend in others - especially if compulsions aligned with group needs.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-044
Work: Unknown
Title: OCD as Misapplied Boundary-Maintenance System

Position:
In modern abstract, crowded, digital world, machinery that maintained physical/moral boundaries has no natural object. So turns inward, fixates on trivialities, creates imagined scenarios to defuse through ritual. System isn't broken - it's misapplied, doing its job too well in wrong context.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-045
Work: Unknown
Title: OCD as Sacred Function Misfiring

Position:
You don't get OCD from nowhere - you get it from same architecture that in another life might have made you priest, scout, healer, watchman. Pain is real but mind isn't broken - it's just tuned for world that no longer exists.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-046
Work: Unknown
Title: Economics Not Self-Contained Predictive System

Position:
Economics is not self-contained system that can predict itself. It's downstream of culture, politics, religion, personality, invention. Charismatic leader can redirect nation's economy in week. War, famine, singularity make mockery of best economic models. These events aren't noise - they're constitutive.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-047
Work: Unknown
Title: Economics vs Biology: Probabilistic vs Non-Self-Predictive

Position:
Biology is probabilistic but not arbitrary - state variables constrain future through non-random mechanisms. Economics not even robustly probabilistic. System never was self-predictive to begin with. Not that it's sound but occasionally disrupted - it's that it was never self-predictive.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-048
Work: Unknown
Title: Inca Example: Economics Records But Doesn't Explain Non-Economic Systems

Position:
To predict Inca behavior in 1457, look at 1456 rituals, laws, cosmic beliefs, cosmological metaphors - not marginal utility curves. Economics may record food stores and track trade but won't tell why workers redeployed to sacred site, surplus burned instead of stored, labor restructured to appease eclipse.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-049
Work: Unknown
Title: Serial Killerdom as Specific Cognitive-Behavioral Protocol

Position:
Serial murder is not random violence but premeditated, patterned, highly stylized behavior with limited recurring types (organized/disorganized, visionary/hedonistic, power/mission-oriented). This taxonomic stability suggests it's specific cognitive-behavioral protocol, not generic trauma response.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-050
Work: Unknown
Title: Serial Killerdom Not Modern Invention But Modern Category

Position:
Serial murder has long existed (Gilles de Rais, Elizabeth Báthory, slaughtering priests of empires). What's new isn't behavior but recognition as distinct category - product of modern bureaucratic state with tools to track, name, mythologize recurring patterns.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-051
Work: Unknown
Title: Trauma as Trigger Not Cause of Serial Killing

Position:
Many serial killers had disturbing upbringings but 'trauma = serial killer' doesn't track. Most abuse victims don't become serial murderers. Some notorious killers didn't experience abuse exceeding ordinary dysfunction. Trauma is trigger sparking very particular pre-existing architecture.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-052
Work: Unknown
Title: Serial Killerdom as Evolutionary Spandrel or Vestigial Adaptation

Position:
If behavior is specific, structured, eerily reproducible, must ask where it came from. Evolution repurposes, mutates, experiments with hyper-specialists. Serial killerdom perhaps: spandrel (byproduct of adaptive features), vestigial adaptation, or extreme failure mode of modules serving critical social functions.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-053
Work: Unknown
Title: Serial Killers as Overclocked Predator Mode

Position:
What sets serial killers apart isn't violence but method: they stalk, hunt, blend in, mimic normal social behavior with chilling precision. Not moral deformity but overactivation of predator mode made grotesque by misfiring reward circuits and unregulated internal narratives.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-054
Work: Unknown
Title: Economic Theory as Intellectual Colonization

Position:
When Western-trained economist attempts to manage non-Western economy, doesn't observe or listen but immediately translates: 'What's your interest rate? Marginal productivity? Utility function?' None make sense in native conceptual world, but economist is there to re-code not learn.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: PS-055
Work: Unknown
Title: Flattening Sacred into Economic Data

Position:
Incan administrator describes labor system organized around sacred seasons, familial debt, reciprocal land stewardship. Economist replies: 'Ah yes, non-monetary kinship-based tax structure with redistributive efficiency function.' But that's not what it is - that's just bad translation. The ritual is no longer ritual, sacred no longer sacred.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-CP001
Work: Unknown
Title: The Hypothetico-Deductive Method Has Serious Problems

Position:
The hypothetico-deductive method of scientific confirmation faces significant philosophical difficulties that undermine its status as the primary method of scientific reasoning.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-CP002
Work: Unknown
Title: Values Play an Essential Role in Science

Position:
Value judgments are not eliminable from scientific practice. Science necessarily involves value assumptions that go beyond purely empirical matters.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-CP003
Work: Unknown
Title: Modern Science Has Distinctive Epistemic Features

Position:
Modern scientific method differs fundamentally from pre-modern approaches to knowledge in ways that have important philosophical implications.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-CP004
Work: Unknown
Title: Early Modern Scientific Thought Represents Philosophical Breakthrough

Position:
The scientific revolution of the early modern period (Galileo, Newton, etc.) represents a fundamental shift in philosophical thinking about nature and knowledge.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-CP005
Work: Unknown
Title: Global Warming Evidence Is Compelling

Position:
The scientific evidence for anthropogenic climate change is strong enough to warrant serious concern and policy responses.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-CP006
Work: Unknown
Title: Evolution Is Well-Established Scientific Fact

Position:
The theory of evolution by natural selection is supported by overwhelming evidence and is as well-established as any scientific theory.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-CP007
Work: Unknown
Title: Modern Science Risks Faustian Separation from Nature

Position:
Modern science's attempt to rise above and dominate nature (symbolized by Faust) risks losing connection with our natural grounding.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-CP008
Work: Unknown
Title: Neuroscience Can Potentially Increase Happiness

Position:
David Pearce's argument that neuroscience and genetic engineering could dramatically increase human happiness has merit, despite measurement difficulties.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-CP009
Work: Unknown
Title: Subjective Happiness Not Quantifiable But Neural Correlates Are

Position:
While happiness as subjective experience may not be quantifiable, its neural underpinnings (neuron firing patterns, neurotransmitter levels) are quantifiable and manipulable.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-004
Work: Unknown
Title: AI Falsifies Popperian Falsificationism

Position:
AI's success in scientific discovery falsifies Popper's theory that science proceeds primarily through conjecture and refutation. AI systems generate successful theories through pattern matching and inductive generalization, not primarily through bold conjectures and attempts at falsification.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-005
Work: Unknown
Title: Inductive Discovery Precedes Deductive Testing

Position:
Contra Popper, successful scientific discovery requires inductive pattern recognition to generate plausible hypotheses before deductive testing. AI demonstrates that purely conjectural approaches without inductive guidance are ineffective.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-006
Work: Unknown
Title: Reverse Brain Engineering as Scientific Method

Position:
By building AI systems that replicate cognitive functions, we can infer the computational architecture necessary for those functions. This 'reverse engineering' of the brain through AI construction represents a new and powerful methodology in philosophy of science and cognitive science.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-007
Work: Unknown
Title: AI Falsifies Deductive-Nomological Model of Explanation

Position:
AI's successful explanatory practices falsify the deductive-nomological (covering law) model of explanation. AI generates successful explanations through pattern recognition, analogy, and causal modeling that don't require deduction from universal laws.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-008
Work: Unknown
Title: Causal-Mechanistic Explanation Doesn't Require Universal Laws

Position:
AI demonstrates that causal-mechanistic explanation can be successful without appeal to universal laws. Understanding how something works doesn't require subsuming it under exceptionless generalizations.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-009
Work: Unknown
Title: Explanatory Understanding Through Pattern Recognition

Position:
AI reveals that explanatory understanding can be achieved through recognition of patterns and structural similarities rather than derivation from laws. This suggests explanation is more about grasping relevant relationships than deductive systematization.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-010
Work: Unknown
Title: Laws of Nature Not Confined to Actual Objects

Position:
The scope of natural law is not confined to actual or even possible objects. Many laws hold with respect to classes all of whose members are merely possible or even prohibited by other natural laws.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-011
Work: Unknown
Title: Knowledge of Imperceptibles Identical with Conditional Knowledge

Position:
Knowledge of the imperceptible is identical with knowledge of conditional truth. Knowledge of future, past, possible, and imperceptible present states is always conditional knowledge based on laws.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-012
Work: Unknown
Title: Three Kinds of Imperceptibles

Position:
Physical objects can be imperceptible in three ways: (1) imperceptible due to severed causal processes (objects in other rooms); (2) imperceptible due to size but perceptible with technology (cells, molecules); (3) imperceptible by natural law regardless of technology (photons, subatomic particles).

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-013
Work: Unknown
Title: The Epistemic Function of Natural Law

Position:
Scientists aspire to identify natural laws so they can, when given context-specific information, make true statements about future, past, or possible behavior of contexts. Laws enable conditional prediction and explanation.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-014
Work: Unknown
Title: Science Prioritizes Principles Over Particular Facts

Position:
Any interest science has in a given particular fact is subordinate to its interest in the general principles in terms of which that fact is to be understood. Scientists study particular instances only insofar as they instantiate general laws.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-015
Work: Unknown
Title: Laws May Be Place and Time-Sensitive

Position:
Some natural laws are place- and time-sensitive rather than spatiotemporally invariant. Laws need not hold uniformly across all regions of space-time to be genuine laws.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-016
Work: Unknown
Title: Hume's Regularity Analysis of Causation Is False

Position:
Hume's Regularity Analysis - the view that causation is nothing but constant conjunction, that 'X causes Y' means 'events of type X are regularly followed by events of type Y' - is demonstrably false.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-017
Work: Unknown
Title: Hume-Worlds Observationally Different from Non-Humean Worlds

Position:
A Hume-world (where causation equals regularity with no underlying powers) would be observationally different from our world. The concept of a Hume-world cannot support Hume's analysis.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-018
Work: Unknown
Title: The Deductive-Nomological Model of Explanation Is False

Position:
The Deductive-Nomological (DN) model - which holds that to explain event E is to derive E from natural laws plus antecedent conditions - is fundamentally mistaken. Explanation requires causal knowledge, not merely law-subsumption.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-019
Work: Unknown
Title: DN Viciously Circular via Counterfactual Support

Position:
The DN model is viciously circular if it requires laws to support counterfactuals (as Hempel proposes). Counterfactuals are cryptocausal statements; knowing them requires knowing causes; but knowing causes already provides explanations.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-020
Work: Unknown
Title: Causal Knowledge as Differential Knowledge

Position:
Causal knowledge is differential knowledge - knowledge of what varies with what. To know causes is to know which changes depend on which other changes and in what proportions.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-021
Work: Unknown
Title: Causation as Proportionality Restoration

Position:
Causation is fundamentally proportionality restoration. Effects are proportional to their causes (threshold effects aside). When a force acts on an object, the resulting change is proportional to the force magnitude.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-022
Work: Unknown
Title: Physical Laws as Regularities of Proportion

Position:
Physical laws are regularities of proportion rather than simple universal generalizations. Laws describe how magnitudes vary proportionally with each other rather than stating that all Fs are Gs.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-023
Work: Unknown
Title: Knowledge-Why Equals High-Resolution Knowledge-What

Position:
To have knowledge-why is to have high-resolution knowledge-what. Explanatory knowledge differs from mere descriptive knowledge in degree of detail and specificity, not in kind.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-024
Work: Unknown
Title: The Raven Paradox a By-Product of Regularity Analysis

Position:
The Raven Paradox (that non-black non-ravens confirm 'all ravens are black') is an artifact of the Regularity Analysis of causation. Once causation is properly understood, the paradox dissolves.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-025
Work: Unknown
Title: Determinism Doesn't Entail Complete Predictability

Position:
Determinism (every event has a cause) does not entail complete predictability. Two reasons: (1) interference effects make prediction impossible without infinite precision, and (2) knowledge growth itself cannot be predicted.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-026
Work: Unknown
Title: Implementation-Indeterminism Distinguished from Program-Determinism

Position:
Program-determinism (software-level determinism) is compatible with implementation-indeterminism (hardware-level indeterminism). The same program can be implemented by different physical processes.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-027
Work: Unknown
Title: Truths Not Objects Are Objects of Explanation

Position:
Truths, not objects or states of affairs themselves, are the proper objects of explanation. We explain why propositions are true, not why objects exist (except derivatively).

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-050
Work: Unknown
Title: Probability is causal, not statistical

Position:
When it is said that probability of a computer-malfunction is greater than 0%, the statement being made is to be interpreted CAUSALLY, not statistically. Probability is a function of laws and causal mechanisms, not observed frequencies.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-051
Work: Unknown
Title: Statistics are evidence for probability, not identical with probability

Position:
Statistics are evidence of probabilities; statistics are not themselves probabilities. Frequency Theory (FT) wrongly identifies statistics with probability.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-052
Work: Unknown
Title: W1/W2 thought experiment refutes Frequency Theory

Position:
W1: laws say P(malfunction)=10%, statistics show 10%. W2: same laws, P(malfunction)=10%, but by coincidence statistics show 0%. Frequency Theory wrongly says P(W2)=0% but P(W1)=10%. Both actually have P=10% (determined by laws).

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-053
Work: Unknown
Title: Smoking-cancer example refutes Frequency Theory

Position:
In a world with our biological laws but where by coincidence no smoker gets cancer, Frequency Theory says P(cancer|smoking)=0%. Wrong. P(cancer|smoking) = same as our world (determined by biological laws), regardless of coincidental statistics.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-054
Work: Unknown
Title: Same laws entail same probabilities regardless of statistics

Position:
Worlds with identical laws of nature have identical probabilities, regardless of any statistical divergences caused by coincidence.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: SCI-055
Work: Unknown
Title: Different causal/nomic structures entail different probabilities

Position:
If two universes have different causal/nomic structures (different laws), they have different probabilities, even if their event-sequences are observationally identical.

================================================================================
DOMAIN: VIRTUE_THEORY (5 positions)
================================================================================

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: VIRTUE-001
Work: WORK-010
Title: Superior Person's Vigilant Stability

Position:
The superior person maintains stable, centered attitude while being appropriately responsive to changing circumstances. 'When resting in safety, does not forget danger may come. When secure, does not overlook possibility of ruin. When orderly, knows disorder may come. Therefore, when disaster strikes, is ready.'

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: VIRTUE-002
Work: WORK-010
Title: Judicious Speech as Virtue

Position:
The superior person is careful about what they say and how they say it; they do not speak loosely. Carefulness in speech reflects carefulness in thought and respect for words' consequences.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: VIRTUE-003
Work: WORK-010
Title: Practice-Preaching Unity

Position:
The superior person practices what they preach and either reconciles themselves to their situation or changes it. They are never idle.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: VIRTUE-004
Work: WORK-010
Title: Moral Courage as Essential Virtue

Position:
To know what you must do and still not do it shows lack of moral courage, which is the worst sin. Excellence requires moral courage, not merely will power.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: VIRTUE-005
Work: WORK-010
Title: Earnest Striving Constitutes Achievement

Position:
If you earnestly try to be a superior person, you are, for that very reason, on your way to being such a person. The sincere attempt itself constitutes progress toward the goal.
